21/06/24, 11:59â€¯am - +91 98071 13102: CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` FUNCTION `fine_call`(mem INT) RETURNS int
    DETERMINISTIC
BEGIN
    DECLARE dif INT;
    DECLARE fin INT;
    DECLARE var_isu DATE;
    DECLARE var_ret DATE;

    -- Select issue date and return date into variables
    SELECT issue_date, return_date INTO var_isu, var_ret
    FROM book_issue 
    WHERE mcode = mem;

    -- Calculate the difference in days between return date and issue date
    SET dif = DATEDIFF(var_ret, var_isu);

    -- If the difference is more than 7 days, calculate the fine
    IF dif > 7 THEN
        SET fin = (dif - 7) * 10;
    ELSE
        SET fin = 0;
    END IF;

    RETURN fin;
END

14/10/24, 11:49â€¯am - Tanisha Idnani SCIT: Greetings SCIT students !

We are pleased to open applications at *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune* for the *Finlatics Business Analyst Experience Program*, an *online Live Project* that helps you gain work experience in *data-driven decision making*. 

*No pre-requisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of the program and all necessary *training* on data-driven decision-making & *Power BI* will be imparted on the program.

To apply, students can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch with them:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba_application?src=scitw

*Benefits* post completion: 
* *Certificate of Work Experience*
* *Letter of Recommendation*

The program will also have *live sessions* to cover additional business cases. 

*Program Duration* : 1 month / 2 months (on student choice)

The program uses a *case study-driven approach*, where you will *assess business projects* and *solve problems* using models used by leading firms like *McKinsey*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on actual *sales data* to gain insights.

*Program Start*: Flexible on student choice. Can be started *post exams*. 

This project is running at *leading campuses* including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Madras* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

*Time Commitment*: 2 - 4 hours per week

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee of Rs. 1999 + GST / 2999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*:  A *fee waiver of 15 - 25%* shall be given to all *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune*  students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This waiver will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1690 + GST / Rs. 2199 + GST. 

To be eligible for the fee waiver, kindly apply through the abovementioned link only.

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement. 

Best regards,
Team Finlatics

25/10/24, 2:22â€¯pm - Tanisha Idnani SCIT: Greetings SCIT students !

Please note that application are open at *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune* for the *Finlatics Business Analyst Experience Program*, an *online Live Project* that helps you gain work experience in *data-driven decision making*. 

*No pre-requisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of the program and all necessary *training* on data-driven decision-making & *Power BI* will be imparted on the program.

To apply, students can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch with them:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba_application?src=scitwr

*Benefits* post completion: 
* *Certificate of Work Experience*
* *Letter of Recommendation*

The program will also have *live sessions* to cover additional business cases. 

*Program Duration* : 1 month / 2 months (on student choice)

The program uses a *case study-driven approach*, where you will *assess business projects* and *solve problems* using models used by leading firms like *McKinsey*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on actual *sales data* to gain insights.

*Program Start*: Flexible on student choice. Can be started *post exams*. 

This project is running at *leading campuses* including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Madras* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

*Time Commitment*: 2 - 4 hours per week

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee of Rs. 1999 + GST / 2999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*:  A *fee waiver of 15 - 25%* shall be given to all *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune*  students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This waiver will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1690 + GST / Rs. 2199 + GST. 

To be eligible for the fee waiver, kindly apply through the abovementioned link only.

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement. 

Best regards,
Team Finlatics

*Program Start*: Flexible on student choice. Can be started *post exams*. 

This project is running at *leading campuses* including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Madras* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

18/12/24, 1:13â€¯pm - Tanisha Idnani SCIT: Greetings SCIT students!

We are pleased to open applications at *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune* for the *Finlatics Startup Strategist Experience Program*, an *online Live Project* that helps you gain *work experience* in *building, launching & scaling a start-up*.

On this project, you'll work on start-up ideas across sectors like *fintech, digital media & OTT* and *sustainable & consumer tech* to develop business models, launch & financing strategies. 

This project also runs at *IIT Bombay*, *IIT Delhi*, *IIT Madras* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

On completing, you'll get: 
- *Certificate of Work Experience*
- *Letter of Recommendation*

You can apply via the link below and we'll get in touch:

https://www.finlatics.com/ssep_application?src=scitw

*No prerequisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of this project. Training will be a part of the project itself. 

*Project Duration* : 1 month / 2 months (on your choice)

*Project Start*: Flexible on your schedule. 

You can also take a *break* for exams, assignments, or personal commitments and take an *extension* if you cannot complete it within the duration. 

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee: Rs. 1999 + GST

*Fee Waiver* : A *fee waiver of 25%* shall be given to all *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune* students on the abovementioned fee. This will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1499 + GST. 

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement,

Team Finlatics
